• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期转分钟函数 : minute</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: minute (string date)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回日期中的分钟。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select minute('2011-12-08 10:03:01') from dual;</div>

3</div>
</div>

• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期转秒函数 : second</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: second (string date)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回日期中的秒。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select second('2011-12-08 10:03:01') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
1</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">

• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期转周函数 : weekofyear</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: weekofyear (string date)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回日期在当前的周数。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select weekofyear('2011-12-08 10:03:01') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
49</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期比较函数 : datediff</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: datediff(string enddate, string startdate)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回结束日期减去开始日期的天数。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select datediff('2012-12-08','2012-05-09') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
213</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期增加函数 : date_add</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: date_add(string startdate, int days)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回开始日期startdate增加days天后的日期。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select date_add('2012-12-08',10) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
2012-12-18</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期减少函数 : date_sub</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: date_sub (string startdate, int days)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回开始日期startdate减少days天后的日期。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select date_sub('2012-12-08',10) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
2012-11-28</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">

<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•If函数: if</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•非空查找函数: COALESCE</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•条件判断函数：CASE</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">If 函数 : if</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: if(boolean testCondition, T valueTrue, T valueFalseOrNull)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: T</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明:  当条件testCondition为TRUE时，返回valueTrue；否则返回valueFalseOrNull</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select if(1=2,100,200) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
200</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select if(1=1,100,200) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
100</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">非空查找函数 : COALESCE</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: COALESCE(T v1, T v2, …)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: T</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明:  返回参数中的第一个非空值；如果所有值都为NULL，那么返回NULL</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select COALESCE(null,'100','50′) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
100</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px"><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">条件判断函数：</span></span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px"><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">CASE</span></span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">语法</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">: CASE a WHEN b THEN c [WHEN d THEN e]* [ELSE f] END</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">返回值</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">: T</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">说明：如果</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">a</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">等于</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">b</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">，那么返回</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">c</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">；如果</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">a</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">等于</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">d</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">，那么返回</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">e</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">；否则返回</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">f</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">举例：</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">hive&gt; Select case 100 when 50 then 'tom' when 100 then 'mary' else 'tim' </span><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">end from dual;</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">mary</span></div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px"> </span></div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:16px; font-weight:bold">第六部分：字符串函数</span></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•字符串长度函数：length</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•字符串反转函数：reverse</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•字符串连接函数：concat</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 带分隔符字符串连接函数：concat_ws</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 字符串截取函数：substr,substring</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 字符串截取函数：substr,substring</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 字符串转大写函数：upper,ucase</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 字符串转小写函数：lower,lcase</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 去空格函数：trim</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 左边去空格函数：ltrim</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 右边去空格函数：rtrim</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•正则表达式替换函数：regexp_replace</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•正则表达式解析函数：regexp_extract</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•URL解析函数：parse_url</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•json解析函数：get_json_object</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•空格字符串函数：space</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•重复字符串函数：repeat</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•首字符ascii函数：ascii</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•左补足函数：lpad</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•右补足函数：rpad</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•分割字符串函数: split</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•集合查找函数: find_in_set</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串长度函数： length</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: length(string A)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A的长度</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select length('abcedfg') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
7</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串反转函数： reverse</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: reverse(string A)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A的反转结果</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select reverse(abcedfg’) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
gfdecba</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串连接函数： concat</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: concat(string A, string B…)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回输入字符串连接后的结果，支持任意个输入字符串</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select concat(‘abc’,'def’,'gh’) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
abcdefgh</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">带分隔符字符串连接函数： concat_ws</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: concat_ws(string SEP, string A, string B…)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回输入字符串连接后的结果，SEP表示各个字符串间的分隔符</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select concat_ws(',','abc','def','gh') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
abc,def,gh</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串截取函数： substr,substring</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: substr(string A, int start),substring(string A, int start)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A从start位置到结尾的字符串</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select substr('abcde',3) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
cde</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select substring('abcde',3) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
cde</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt;  select substr('abcde',-1) from dual;  （和ORACLE相同）</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
e</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串截取函数： substr,substring</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: substr(string A, int start, int len),substring(string A, int start, int len)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A从start位置开始，长度为len的字符串</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select substr('abcde',3,2) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
cd</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select substring('abcde',3,2) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
cd</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt;select substring('abcde',-2,2) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
de</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串转大写函数： upper,ucase</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: upper(string A) ucase(string A)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A的大写格式</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select upper('abSEd') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
ABSED</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select ucase('abSEd') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
ABSED</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串转小写函数： lower,lcase</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: lower(string A) lcase(string A)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A的小写格式</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select lower('abSEd') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
absed</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select lcase('abSEd') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
absed</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">去空格函数： trim</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: trim(string A)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：去除字符串两边的空格</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select trim(' abc ') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
abc</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">左边去空格函数： ltrim</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: ltrim(string A)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：去除字符串左边的空格</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select ltrim(' abc ') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
abc</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">

• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">右边去空格函数： rtrim</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: rtrim(string A)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">

• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">正则表达式替换函数： regexp_replace</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: regexp_replace(string A, string B, string C)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：将字符串A中的符合java正则表达式B的部分替换为C。注意，在有些情况下要使用转义字符,类似oracle中的regexp_replace函数。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select regexp_replace('foobar', 'oo|ar', '') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
fb</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">正则表达式解析函数： regexp_extract</span></div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: regexp_extract(string subject, string pattern, int index)</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：将字符串subject按照pattern正则表达式的规则拆分，返回index指定的字符。</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select regexp_extract('foothebar', 'foo(.*?)(bar)', 1) from dual;</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
the</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select regexp_extract('foothebar', 'foo(.*?)(bar)', 2) from dual;</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
bar</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select regexp_extract('foothebar', 'foo(.*?)(bar)', 0) from dual;</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
foothebar</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">注意，在有些情况下要使用转义字符，下面的等号要用双竖线转 义，这是 java 正则表达式的规则。</span></div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
select data_field,</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
regexp_extract(data_field,'.*?bgStart\\=([^&amp;]+)',1) as aaa,</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
regexp_extract(data_field,'.*?contentLoaded_headStart\\=([^&amp;]+)',1) as bbb,</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
regexp_extract(data_field,'.*?AppLoad2Req\\=([^&amp;]+)',1) as ccc</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
from pt_nginx_loginlog_st</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
where pt = '2012-03-26' limit 2;</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">URL 解析函数： parse_url</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: parse_url(string urlString, string partToExtract [, string keyToExtract])</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回URL中指定的部分。partToExtract的有效值为：HOST, PATH, QUERY, REF, PROTOCOL, AUTHORITY, FILE, and USERINFO.</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select parse_url('http://facebook.com/path1/p.php?k1=v1&amp;k2=v2#Ref1', 'HOST') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
facebook.com</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select parse_url('http://facebook.com/path1/p.php?k1=v1&amp;k2=v2#Ref1', 'QUERY', 'k1') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
v1</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">json 解析函数： get_json_object</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: get_json_object(string json_string, string path)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：解析json的字符串json_string,返回path指定的内容。如果输入的json字符串无效，那么返回NULL。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select  get_json_object('{"store":</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
&gt;   {"fruit":\[{"weight":8,"type":"apple"},{"weight":9,"type":"pear"}],</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
&gt;    "bicycle":{"price":19.95,"color":"red"}</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
&gt;   },</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
&gt;  "email":"amy@only_for_json_udf_test.net",</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
&gt;  "owner":"amy"</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
&gt; }</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
&gt; ','$.owner') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
amy</div>
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">空格字符串函数： space</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: space(int n)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回长度为n的字符串</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select space(10) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select length(space(10)) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
10</div>
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">重复字符串函数： repeat</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: repeat(string str, int n)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回重复n次后的str字符串</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select repeat('abc',5) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
abcabcabcabcabc</div>
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">首字符 ascii 函数： ascii</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: ascii(string str)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串str第一个字符的ascii码</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select ascii('abcde') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
97</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">左补足函数： lpad</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: lpad(string str, int len, string pad)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：将str进行用pad进行左补足到len位</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select lpad('abc',10,'td') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
tdtdtdtabc</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">注意：与 GP ， ORACLE 不同， pad 不能默认</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">右补足函数： rpad</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: rpad(string str, int len, string pad)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：将str进行用pad进行右补足到len位</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select rpad('abc',10,'td') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
abctdtdtdt</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">分割字符串函数 : split</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法:  split(string str, string pat)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值:  array</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 按照pat字符串分割str，会返回分割后的字符串数组</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select split('abtcdtef','t') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
["ab","cd","ef"]</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">集合查找函数 : find_in_set</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: find_in_set(string str, string strList)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回str在strlist第一次出现的位置，strlist是用逗号分割的字符串。如果没有找该str字符，则返回0</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select find_in_set('ab','ef,ab,de') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
2</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select find_in_set('at','ef,ab,de') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
0</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:16px; font-weight:bold">第七部分：集合统计函数</span></div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•个数统计函数: count</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•总和统计函数: sum</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•平均值统计函数: avg</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 最小值统计函数: min</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•最大值统计函数: max</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">个数统计函数 : count</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: count(*), count(expr), count(DISTINCT expr[, expr_.])</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: count(*)统计检索出的行的个数，包括NULL值的行；count(expr)返回指定字段的非空值的个数；count(DISTINCT expr[, expr_.])返回指定字段的不同的非空值的个数</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select count(*) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
20</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select count(distinct t) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
10</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">总和统计函数 : sum</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: sum(col), sum(DISTINCT col)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: sum(col)统计结果集中col的相加的结果；sum(DISTINCT col)统计结果中col不同值相加的结果</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select sum(t) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
100</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select sum(distinct t) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
70</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">平均值统计函数 : avg</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: avg(col), avg(DISTINCT col)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: avg(col)统计结果集中col的平均值；avg(DISTINCT col)统计结果中col不同值相加的平均值</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select avg(t) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
50</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select avg (distinct t) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
30</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">最小值统计函数 : min</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: min(col)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 统计结果集中col字段的最小值</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select min(t) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
20</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">最大值统计函数 : max</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: maxcol)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 统计结果集中col字段的最大值</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select max(t) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
120</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:16px; font-weight:bold">第八部分：符合类型构建操作</span></div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•Map类型构建: map</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•Struct类型构建: struct</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•array类型构建: array</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">Map 类型构建 : map</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: map (key1, value1, key2, value2, …)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：根据输入的key和value对构建map类型</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; Create table alex_test as select map('100','tom','200','mary') as t from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; describe alex_test;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
t       map&lt;string,string&gt;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select t from alex_test;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
{"100":"tom","200":"mary"}</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">Struct 类型构建 : struct</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: struct(val1, val2, val3, …)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：根据输入的参数构建结构体struct类型</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; create table alex_test as select struct('tom','mary','tim') as t from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; describe alex_test;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
t       struct&lt;col1:string,col2:string,col3:string&gt;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select t from alex_test;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
{"col1":"tom","col2":"mary","col3":"tim"}</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">array 类型构建 : array</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: array(val1, val2, …)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：根据输入的参数构建数组array类型</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; create table alex_test as select array("tom","mary","tim") as t from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; describe alex_test;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
t       array&lt;string&gt;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select t from alex_test;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
["tom","mary","tim"]</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:16px; font-weight:bold">第九部分：复杂类型访问操作</span></div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•array类型访问: A[n]</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•map类型访问: M[key]</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•struct类型访问: S.x</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">array 类型访问 : A[n]</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: A[n]</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
操作类型: A为array类型，n为int类型</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回数组A中的第n个变量值。数组的起始下标为0。比如，A是个值为['foo', 'bar']的数组类型，那么A[0]将返回'foo',而A[1]将返回'bar'</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; create table alex_test as select array("tom","mary","tim") as t from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select t[0],t[1],t[2] from alex_test;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
tom     mary    tim</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">map 类型访问 : M[key]</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: M[key]</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
操作类型: M为map类型，key为map中的key值</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回map类型M中，key值为指定值的value值。比如，M是值为{'f' -&gt; 'foo', 'b' -&gt; 'bar', 'all' -&gt; 'foobar'}的map类型，那么M['all']将会返回'foobar'</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; Create table alex_test as select map('100','tom','200','mary') as t from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select t['200'],t['100'] from alex_test;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
mary    tom</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">struct 类型访问 : S.x</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: S.x</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
操作类型: S为struct类型</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回结构体S中的x字段。比如，对于结构体struct foobar {int foo, int bar}，foobar.foo返回结构体中的foo字段</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; create table alex_test as select struct('tom','mary','tim') as t from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; describe alex_test;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
t       struct&lt;col1:string,col2:string,col3:string&gt;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select t.col1,t.col3 from alex_test;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
tom     tim</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:16px; font-weight:bold">第十部分：复杂类型长度统计函数</span></div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•Map类型长度函数: size(Map&lt;K.V&gt;)</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•array类型长度函数: size(Array&lt;T&gt;)</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•类型转换函数</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
  </div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">Map 类型长度函数 : size(Map&lt;K.V&gt;)</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: size(Map&lt;K.V&gt;)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回map类型的长度</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select size(map('100','tom','101','mary')) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
2</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">array 类型长度函数 : size(Array&lt;T&gt;)</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: size(Array&lt;T&gt;)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回array类型的长度</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select size(array('100','101','102','103')) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
4</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">类型转换函数</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
类型转换函数: cast</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: cast(expr as &lt;type&gt;)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: Expected "=" to follow "type"</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回array类型的长度</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select cast(1 as bigint) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
1</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<p style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:14px; line-height:1.5em">
