• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">对数函数 : log</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: log(double base, double a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回以base为底的a的对数</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select log(4,256) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
4.0</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">幂运算函数 : pow</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: pow(double a, double p)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回a的p次幂</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select pow(2,4) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
16.0</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">幂运算函数 : power</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: power(double a, double p)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回a的p次幂,与pow功能相同</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select power(2,4) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
16.0</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">开平方函数 : sqrt</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: sqrt(double a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回a的平方根</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select sqrt(16) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
4.0</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">二进制函数 : bin</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: bin(BIGINT a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回a的二进制代码表示</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select bin(7) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
111</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">十六进制函数 : hex</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: hex(BIGINT a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 如果变量是int类型，那么返回a的十六进制表示；如果变量是string类型，则返回该字符串的十六进制表示</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select hex(17) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
11</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select hex(‘abc’) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
616263</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">反转十六进制函数 : unhex</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: unhex(string a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回该十六进制字符串所代码的字符串</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select unhex(‘616263’) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
abc</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select unhex(‘11’) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
-</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select unhex(616263) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
abc</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">进制转换函数 : conv</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: conv(BIGINT num, int from_base, int to_base)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 将数值num从from_base进制转化到to_base进制</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select conv(17,10,16) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
11</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select conv(17,10,2) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
10001</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">绝对值函数 : abs</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: abs(double a)   abs(int a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double        int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回数值a的绝对值</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select abs(-3.9) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
3.9</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select abs(10.9) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
10.9</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">正取余函数 : pmod</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: pmod(int a, int b),pmod(double a, double b)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回正的a除以b的余数</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select pmod(9,4) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
1</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select pmod(-9,4) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
3</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">正弦函数 : sin</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: sin(double a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回a的正弦值</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select sin(0.8) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
0.7173560908995228</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">反正弦函数 : asin</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: asin(double a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回a的反正弦值</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select asin(0.7173560908995228) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
0.8</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">余弦函数 : cos</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: cos(double a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回a的余弦值</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select cos(0.9) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
0.6216099682706644</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">反余弦函数 : acos</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: acos(double a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回a的反余弦值</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select acos(0.6216099682706644) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
0.9</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">positive 函数 : positive</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: positive(int a), positive(double a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回a</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select positive(-10) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
-10</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select positive(12) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
12</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">negative 函数 : negative</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: negative(int a), negative(double a)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int double</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回-a</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select negative(-5) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
5</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select negative(8) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
-8</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:16px; font-weight:bold">第四部分：日期函数</span></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•UNIX时间戳转日期函数: from_unixtime</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 获取当前UNIX时间戳函数: unix_timestamp</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•日期转UNIX时间戳函数: unix_timestamp</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 指定格式日期转UNIX时间戳函数: unix_timestamp</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•日期时间转日期函数: to_date</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•日期转年函数: year</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 日期转月函数: month</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 日期转天函数: day</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 日期转小时函数: hour</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 日期转分钟函数: minute</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 日期转秒函数: second</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 日期转周函数: weekofyear</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 日期比较函数: datediff</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 日期增加函数: date_add</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 日期减少函数: date_sub</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">UNIX 时间戳转日期函数 : from_unixtime</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: from_unixtime(bigint unixtime[, string format])</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 转化UNIX时间戳（从1970-01-01 00:00:00 UTC到指定时间的秒数）到当前时区的时间格式</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select from_unixtime(1323308943,'yyyyMMdd') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
20111208</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">获取当前 UNIX 时间戳函数 : unix_timestamp</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: unix_timestamp()</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: bigint</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 获得当前时区的UNIX时间戳</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select unix_timestamp() from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
1323309615</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期转 UNIX 时间戳函数 : unix_timestamp</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: unix_timestamp(string date)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: bigint</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 转换格式为"yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"的日期到UNIX时间戳。如果转化失败，则返回0。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select unix_timestamp('2011-12-07 13:01:03') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
1323234063</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">指定格式日期转 UNIX 时间戳函数 : unix_timestamp</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: unix_timestamp(string date, string pattern)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: bigint</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 转换pattern格式的日期到UNIX时间戳。如果转化失败，则返回0。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select unix_timestamp('20111207 13:01:03','yyyyMMdd HH:mm:ss') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
1323234063</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期时间转日期函数 : to_date</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: to_date(string timestamp)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回日期时间字段中的日期部分。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select to_date('2011-12-08 10:03:01') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
2011-12-08</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期转年函数 : year</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: year(string date)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回日期中的年。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select year('2011-12-08 10:03:01') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
2011</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select year('2012-12-08') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
2012</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期转月函数 : month</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: month (string date)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回日期中的月份。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select month('2011-12-08 10:03:01') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
12</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select month('2011-08-08') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
8</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期转天函数 : day</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: day (string date)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回日期中的天。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select day('2011-12-08 10:03:01') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
8</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select day('2011-12-24') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
24</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期转小时函数 : hour</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: hour (string date)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回日期中的小时。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select hour('2011-12-08 10:03:01') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
10</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期转分钟函数 : minute</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: minute (string date)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回日期中的分钟。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select minute('2011-12-08 10:03:01') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
3</div>
</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期转秒函数 : second</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: second (string date)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回日期中的秒。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select second('2011-12-08 10:03:01') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
1</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期转周函数 : weekofyear</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: weekofyear (string date)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回日期在当前的周数。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select weekofyear('2011-12-08 10:03:01') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
49</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期比较函数 : datediff</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: datediff(string enddate, string startdate)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回结束日期减去开始日期的天数。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select datediff('2012-12-08','2012-05-09') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
213</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期增加函数 : date_add</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: date_add(string startdate, int days)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回开始日期startdate增加days天后的日期。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select date_add('2012-12-08',10) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
2012-12-18</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">日期减少函数 : date_sub</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: date_sub (string startdate, int days)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明: 返回开始日期startdate减少days天后的日期。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select date_sub('2012-12-08',10) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
2012-11-28</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:16px; font-weight:bold">第五部分：条件函数</span></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•If函数: if</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•非空查找函数: COALESCE</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•条件判断函数：CASE</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">If 函数 : if</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: if(boolean testCondition, T valueTrue, T valueFalseOrNull)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: T</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明:  当条件testCondition为TRUE时，返回valueTrue；否则返回valueFalseOrNull</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select if(1=2,100,200) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
200</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select if(1=1,100,200) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
100</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">非空查找函数 : COALESCE</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: COALESCE(T v1, T v2, …)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: T</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明:  返回参数中的第一个非空值；如果所有值都为NULL，那么返回NULL</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select COALESCE(null,'100','50′) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
100</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px"><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">条件判断函数：</span></span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px"><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">CASE</span></span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">语法</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">: CASE a WHEN b THEN c [WHEN d THEN e]* [ELSE f] END</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">返回值</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">: T</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">说明：如果</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">a</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">等于</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">b</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">，那么返回</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">c</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">；如果</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">a</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">等于</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">d</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">，那么返回</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">e</span> <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">；否则返回</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">f</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">举例：</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">hive&gt; Select case 100 when 50 then 'tom' when 100 then 'mary' else 'tim' </span><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">end from dual;</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">mary</span></div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px"> </span></div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:16px; font-weight:bold">第六部分：字符串函数</span></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•字符串长度函数：length</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•字符串反转函数：reverse</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•字符串连接函数：concat</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 带分隔符字符串连接函数：concat_ws</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 字符串截取函数：substr,substring</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 字符串截取函数：substr,substring</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 字符串转大写函数：upper,ucase</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 字符串转小写函数：lower,lcase</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 去空格函数：trim</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 左边去空格函数：ltrim</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• 右边去空格函数：rtrim</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•正则表达式替换函数：regexp_replace</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•正则表达式解析函数：regexp_extract</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•URL解析函数：parse_url</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•json解析函数：get_json_object</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•空格字符串函数：space</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•重复字符串函数：repeat</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•首字符ascii函数：ascii</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•左补足函数：lpad</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•右补足函数：rpad</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•分割字符串函数: split</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•集合查找函数: find_in_set</div>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串长度函数： length</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: length(string A)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: int</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A的长度</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select length('abcedfg') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
7</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串反转函数： reverse</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: reverse(string A)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A的反转结果</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select reverse(abcedfg’) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
gfdecba</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串连接函数： concat</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: concat(string A, string B…)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回输入字符串连接后的结果，支持任意个输入字符串</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select concat(‘abc’,'def’,'gh’) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
abcdefgh</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">带分隔符字符串连接函数： concat_ws</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: concat_ws(string SEP, string A, string B…)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回输入字符串连接后的结果，SEP表示各个字符串间的分隔符</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select concat_ws(',','abc','def','gh') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
abc,def,gh</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串截取函数： substr,substring</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: substr(string A, int start),substring(string A, int start)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A从start位置到结尾的字符串</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select substr('abcde',3) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
cde</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select substring('abcde',3) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
cde</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt;  select substr('abcde',-1) from dual;  （和ORACLE相同）</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
e</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串截取函数： substr,substring</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: substr(string A, int start, int len),substring(string A, int start, int len)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A从start位置开始，长度为len的字符串</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select substr('abcde',3,2) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
cd</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select substring('abcde',3,2) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
cd</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt;select substring('abcde',-2,2) from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
de</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串转大写函数： upper,ucase</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: upper(string A) ucase(string A)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A的大写格式</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select upper('abSEd') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
ABSED</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select ucase('abSEd') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
ABSED</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• <span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-size:12px">字符串转小写函数： lower,lcase</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
语法: lower(string A) lcase(string A)</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
返回值: string</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
说明：返回字符串A的小写格式</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
举例：</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select lower('abSEd') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
absed</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; select lcase('abSEd') from dual;</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
absed</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; font-size:12px; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
